 The woman's leg was badly injured as her 'mistress' Shamina Yusuf dragged her from the cup and killed her
 rapat main kaha gaya he ki haalanki us samay koi karrwai nahi kii gai, kyonki mahila ko iske bare main kisi ko bataane ke liye dhamkaaya gaya tha
 The woman escaped after more than two years, but returned to other relatives of the family to get her passport
 mahila ke vakil ne adaalat ko bataaya ki mahila saint johns wood main ek kamare vaale makaan main rahati thi or kasaai, ankarta balapovi ne uske saath kai baar dushkarm kiya
 The woman somehow escaped and her case was handed over to the trafficking unit of Scotland Yard Police in England
 tippaniyan Optician Balaram Oberoi and Secretary Yusuf were convicted for assaulting the woman
 oberoi ko jaan se maarane kii dhamkee dene kaa bhi doshi paaya gaya
 Butcher, Balapovi, was found guilty of rape
 unhen agle maheene sajaa sunai jaaegi
 Two other defendants were released
 peedita abhi marpet ke kaaran itani chotil he ki use wheelchair kaa sahaara lenaa pad rahaa he
 According to the newspaper 'the Independent', the woman requested assistance from the Hertfordshire Police as well as several charitable organizations and other government agencies
 lekin police ne jab bhi mahila se baatcheet kii to mahila ke saath abhadrata karne vaale ek rasukhdaar vyakti ko hi dubhashiya banaaya gaya
 Each time the woman is handed over to her 'owner' and further harassed to discredit the owner's family, she is threatened that she will be buried in the back garden
 mahila ko teen varsh se adhik samay tak pratadit karne ke aarope main teen logon ko doshi tehraaya gaya
 One of the three persons is an optician, a butcher and a secretary
 samachar patr kii rapat ke anusaar, mahila ko teenon pariwaron ke bich aadan-pradaan kiya jaataa or gulam kii tarah rakhaa jaataa
 They had confiscated the woman's passport and did not even give the woman a single penny
 adalati dastavej ke anusaar mahila jab bhi bhagkar police ke paas sahaayta ke liye gai, uski yachana ko police ne nazarandaaj kar diya
 This happened at least 12 times

 andhra pradesh ko vishesh rajya kaa darja dene kii maang ko lekar telugu desham party ke rashtriya janatantric gathbandhan se alag hone ke baad bhaajapa adhyaksh amit shah ne aaj tedepa pramukh or andhra pradesh ke mukhyamantri ko patr likhakar is faisle ko raajnneeti se prerit or ekatarfa qaraar diya
 Shah said that the commitment of the Modi government towards the development of Andhra Pradesh is firm and no one can question it
 endie se alag hone ke naidu ke faisle ko durbhypurna qaraar dete hue shah ne patr main kaha ki yah faisla puri tarah se raajnneeti se prerit he or isamen pradesh ke vikaas ko darkinar kiya gaya he
 Shah wrote that BJP has always believed in the politics of development and working and this is our source of inspiration
 shah ne likhaa he ki andhra pradesh ke bantwaare se lekar aaj tak bhaajapa ne hameshaa andhra pradesh ke logon kii aawaaj ko uthaaya he or logon ke hiton ke liye kaam kiya he
 We constantly think about the interest of the Telugu people and the Telugu state
 congress ne pradesh ke bantwaare main logon ke hiton kaa khyal nahin rakhaa jisaki vajah se logon ko mushkil kaa saamana karnaa padataa he
 The Congress did not take care of the sentiments of the people during the Partition

 Did they know what the price of 2007 is, if it is not known, why not write it in the blog
 jabaki ve yahi sawaal rahul gandhi se blog main karte hai ki kya unhen 2007 main tay keemat kaa pataa he
 Jaitley answers how a private company entered the deal
 kehete hai ki upie ke samay hi shart bani thi ki jo mul nirmaataa company he wo bharat main kalpurzon kii aapurti yaa rakrakhaav ke liye khud se bhartiya company ko saajheedaar bana sakati he
 It has nothing to do with the government
 lekin iskaa jawaab nahin mila ki rafaal banane vaali dasso avishan company kyon ek aisi company ko saajheedaar banaaegi, jiskaa is kshetra main anubhav kaaphi nayaa he or aarope he ki vah company kuch hi maheene pehle vajood main ai he
 Jaitley does not touch this aspect
 jetali ne apane blog main is baat kaa jawaab diya he ki deal sin se pehle 14 maheene tak Price Negotiation Committee or Contract Negotiation Committee ne is par vichaar-vimarsh kiya he

 After North Korea's threat of a nuclear attack, the US conducted maneuvers to counter the attack
 ye yuddhayas neuyork shahar ke baahar manahaton main kiya gaya
 The drill was named Operation Gotham Shield
 darasal drill kaa makasad ye dekhnaa tha ki yadi 10 kiloton kaa newclear bam girtaa he to kaise local immergency or management team isse nipategi
 Emergency management director of New Jersey Jeffrey Paul posted photos of the drill on Facebook
 ye drill brihaspativaar tak jari rahegi
 Explain at the Lincoln Tunnel that on Tuesday, on the occasion of the 85th anniversary of its army, North Korea manned its east coast with large arms
 media reports ke mutabik newclear hamale ke khatre ko dekhte hue new jersey ke paas linkan tunnel ke paas ek dhamaakaa bhi kiya gaya
 Not only this, the medical center of Heineksek Universiti also participated in this drill
 jaifari ke mutabik aaj kareeb hajaaron log metlife stadium main icttha hue
 They were acting to seek help after the attack
 hamaara mishan tha in sabhi ko treetment dena, yadi koi buree tarah se ghayal he to use hospital tak pahunchaana
 There was no real patient in this drill
 iske liye kareeb 30 maas care centre bhi taiyaar kiye gaye the
 According to media reports, Frank Montaz, the Chief of Race, North Hudson, has said that we are testing our capabilities through this
 hamen ummid he aisa hamalaa kabhi nahin hoga lekin hamen kisi bhi paristhiti ke liye taiyaar rahanaa chahie
 In addition to Manhattan, the drill will take place in Washington and Albany, New York
 9 \ 11 hamale ke baad hui thi aisi hi dricamerica ke jaankaron kaa maananaa he ki ye north korea main bad rahe tanaav ke baad yah drill ek nakli flag oparation ho saktaa he
 According to some experts, even after the 9 / 11 attack, such a drill operation was done
 haalanki adhikariyon ke mutabik ye drill kai samay se chali aa rahi he
 It is not for any specific threat
 adhikariyon ne kaha ki isse pehle bhi kai tuphaanon se nipatane ke liye ham aisi drill alag-alag shaharon main karte rahe hai
 The government has abandoned the idea of bringing an ordinance to amend the Arbitration Act
 sarkaar ke is kadam ko ek tarah se sarkaar dwaara adhyadeshon par adhik nirbharta ko taalane kii koshish ke rup main dekha ja rahaa he
 The President asked, "why is the ordinance hurried?" President Pranab Mukherjee has expressed serious objections to the issuance of ordinances in large numbers
 is adhyadesh ke tahat vanijyik vivaad maamalon main sunwaayee kii adhyakshata kar rahe madhyasthon ke liye maamalon kaa nau maheene main niptaan karnaa anivaary kiye jane kaa praavdhaan karne kaa prastaav he
 The Union Cabinet approved it but it was not sent to the President for approval
 sutron ne kaha ki sarkaar ne ab adhyadesh laane kaa faisla chhod diya he
 Instead, it will bring the Bill for amendment to the Arbitration and Conciliation Act, 1996 in the budget session of Parliament which will begin on 23 February
